- [x] **Phase 23: GDD SDK Domain Primitives — Knowledge Layer SDK, Visual & Token Engines, Distribution** — **Knowledge layer SDK:** intel store (`.design/intel/`) typed reader/writer; knowledge graph (`.planning/graphs/`) typed query layer; skill manifest registry with capability matching; project-local skills (`./.claude/skills/`) auto-discovery; cycle/workstream model. **Visual + token primitives:** image diff primitive (regression baseline drift), screenshot capture orchestration (Playwright + Claude Preview MCP wrapper), visual baseline manager (`.design/baselines/`), design-token reader (multi-source: CSS vars / JS const / Tailwind config / Figma variables), token diff + applier (for darkmode/brand variants). **Pipeline primitives:** `Touches:` analyzer + parallelism decision engine in code (replaces prompt-encoded version from Phase 10.1); audit aggregator (collects findings from N audit-agents, scores, prioritizes); per-stage budget allocator (reads `.design/budget.json`, hard-stops at limits); reference resolver (`type:forms` task → `reference/form-patterns.md`); pause/resume context serializer. **Domain primitives:** NNG heuristic checker (code-level), anti-pattern catalog matcher (regex signature registry), WCAG threshold validator, handoff bundle parser (claude-design-html / claude-design-bundle / manual), spec↔code↔visual triangulation verifier (gates on Phase 16–17 component specs; ships placeholder if not yet landed), git operations primitive (atomic commit, branch state, deviation handling). **Solidify-with-rollback gate:** new `validation:` field on each task in `DESIGN-PLAN.md` (default: repo-level typecheck + build + targeted test from `.design/config.json`); `scripts/lib/design-solidify.mjs` runs after each `design-executor` task commit — on validation failure, auto-reverts the task commit via `git stash` (configurable `rollback_mode: "stash" | "hard" | "none"`, default `"stash"`); writes outcome to the Phase 22 event chain. Turns each task into an atomic commit-or-revert unit; closes today's partial-state problem where a broken task 3 corrupts tasks 4–10 before `/gdd:verify` runs end-of-plan. **JSON output contracts for planner/verifier:** extend `reference/output-contracts/` with `planner-decision.schema.json` + `verifier-decision.schema.json`; agents embed a fenced JSON block between `json` markers at the top of output; `scripts/lib/parse-contract.cjs` validates against schema and returns structured data or actionable error. `/gdd:synthesize` consumes JSON directly instead of regex-parsing 5 parallel mapper markdown outputs — eliminates the silent-drift failure mode when a mapper reformats headings. **Auto-crystallization of repeated Touches: patterns:** `scripts/lib/touches-pattern-miner.cjs` scans `.design/archive/cycle-*/tasks/*.md` after `/gdd:complete-cycle`; when a `Touches:` signature (path-normalized, cycle-slug-stripped) recurs in ≥3 tasks across ≥2 cycles, reflector emits a proposed `./.claude/skills/design-<slug>-conventions/SKILL.md` draft via `/gdd:apply-reflections` with `source: auto-crystallized from cycles [N,M,O]` header. User accepts or rejects — never auto-applied. Promotes execution traces (behavior library) as a complement to genes/capsules (data library). **Distribution:** package as `@hegemonart/gdd-sdk` separate npm package + keep MCP server in plugin. Migration guide for plugin consumers. Headless-mode operations guide. API reference + MCP tools reference. Final regression baseline locks the SDK contract.
- [x] **Phase 23.5: No-Regret Adaptive Layer (INSERTED)** — Turns the passive Phase 22–23 observability + validation infrastructure into a closed self-tuning loop. Three tightly-scoped algorithms sharing one posterior file and one feature flag, **no opt-in shared telemetry required for v1** (solved via informed-prior bootstrap from Anthropic public pricing + GDD agent taxonomy; `Beta(α, β)` priors with `α+β≈10` mean 5–10 local samples shift the posterior — single-user viable). **Bandit router:** `scripts/lib/bandit-router.cjs` — contextual Thompson sampling over `(agent_type, touches_size_bin) → {haiku, sonnet, opus}` with per-arm `Beta(α, β)` posterior at `.design/telemetry/posterior.json`; replaces Phase 10.1 D-13 static tier map when `adaptive_mode: "full"`. **Hedge ensemble:** `scripts/lib/hedge-ensemble.cjs` — AdaNormalHedge (parameter-free Weighted Majority, no manual η) over verifier/checker agents; weights update from solidify-gate outcome as `w[i] *= exp(-η·loss[i])`, verify-stage consensus is weight-thresholded instead of unanimous. **MMR decision-injector rerank:** `scripts/lib/mmr-rerank.cjs` — Maximal Marginal Relevance post-pass on Phase 14.5 top-K surfacing (`λ·relevance − (1−λ)·max_lexical_sim`, hash-based similarity, no embedding API dep, λ=0.7 default); solves the "all 5 injected learnings are about color tokens" failure mode. **Two-stage lexicographic reward** (resolves scalarization-weight tuning as a product decision): `if !solidify_pass: 0 elif user_undo_in_session: 0 else: 1 − λ·normalize(api_cost + ε·wall_time)` — correctness is never traded for cost; `/gsd-undo` = delayed strong negative. **Non-stationarity:** discounted Thompson sampling with per-arm decay `ρ^days_since_last_use` (ρ ≈ 0.988/day, 60-day half-life) for gradual drift + manual `/gdd:bandit-reset --reason "<model-release>"` for abrupt Anthropic model transitions; auto-detection deferred. **Feature flag ladder:** `budget.json.adaptive_mode: "static" | "hedge" | "full"` — three levels so users adopt incrementally (hedge-only is the safest intro since it only affects consensus thresholding, full flips bandit routing on). **Reflector integration:** Phase 22 code-level reflector reads `posterior.json` + hedge weights, proposes `tier_overrides` and weight-threshold diffs via `/gdd:apply-reflections` when single-arm confidence interval tightens below `stddev(Beta(α, β)) < 0.05`. **Deferred (evidence-gated):** hierarchical shared prior (revisit after 20+ cycles of measured single-user convergence), dense-embedding retrieval (revisit if MMR-only miss-rate on `/gdd:recall` exceeds 15%), offline policy evaluation harness (bootstraps naturally from bandit's stochastic logs — D-13 static logging is deterministic so IPS is undefined until Thompson sampling ships). **Explicitly out of scope** (discussed and rejected): HDBSCAN auto-crystallization (data-gated — needs 200+ cycles), BOCPD changepoint detection (reflector covers v1), Personalized PageRank (LLM ranking + MMR cover v1), MinHash/LSH dedup (authority-watcher volume too small), Borda/Kemeny rank aggregation for mapper synthesis (category error — mappers produce orthogonal views, not rankings over the same items), submodular greedy for agent spawn selection (N=4–6, theoretical guarantees irrelevant at this scale). Ships as v1.23.5 (decimal PATCH per versioning scheme — does not shift Phase 24 → v1.24.0). **Depends on**: Phase 22 (event chain + `agent_outcome` events provide reward-signal plumbing), Phase 23 (solidify-with-rollback gate provides binary reward ground truth; JSON output contracts enable structured posterior reads without markdown regex).
- [ ] **Phase 25: Pipeline Hardening — Prototype Gate, Complexity Buckets, Quality Gate, Turn Closeout** — Closes four pipeline gaps surfaced in the post-Phase-24 retrospective: prototyping is structurally orphaned (sketch/spike outputs live in `.design/sketches/<slug>/` and `.design/spikes/<slug>/` with no link back into the pipeline — planner reads neither), router complexity buckets are too coarse (3 buckets collapse `/gdd:help` zero-spawn with `/gdd:scan` single-Sonnet into the same `fast` lane, no signal carries through telemetry), no Lint/Test gate sits between Design and Verify (verify-stage NNG/WCAG/integration checks pass while broken TypeScript or failing tests reach final cycle artifacts), no terminal seam exists at turn-end (events.jsonl has gaps for turns that ended without a tool call; orphan `status: in_progress` states never get checkpointed). **Prototype gate:** new `agents/prototype-gate.md` (Haiku-tier signal-scoring rubric — sketch signals: BRIEF mentions hero/novel surface, DESIGN-CONTEXT gray areas tagged visual/direction, DESIGN.md scan empty, ≥2 D-XX disagree on same surface, interview answers contain "not sure"/"open to"/"??", phase-researcher returned >1 viable pattern; spike signals: plan task `Risk: high` or `Confidence: low`, task touches tech absent from components mapper, required connection probe failed but plan depends on it, task description has "experimental"/"TBD"/"unsure"). Fires after `/gdd:explore` (sketch territory) and after `/gdd:plan` plan-checker (spike territory). Cycle-scoped skip flag (declined-this-cycle never re-asks). New STATE.md `<prototyping>` block schema (`<sketch slug=… cycle=… decision=D-XX status=resolved/>` + `<spike …/>` + `<skipped at=… cycle=… reason=…/>`). `sketch-wrap-up` + `spike-wrap-up` updated to write outcome as a D-XX decision (chosen variant + rationale; spike answer: yes/no/conditional-on-X) and append `<prototyping>` entry. `hooks/gdd-decision-injector.js` reads `<prototyping>` for downstream agent context — sketch outcome becomes a planner constraint, spike answer becomes an executor pre-flight check. **Complexity buckets refinement (S/M/L/XL):** extend router heuristic table at `skills/router/SKILL.md:33` to four buckets — **S** (`/gdd:help`, `/gdd:stats`, `/gdd:note`, single-Haiku skills: skip router itself via deterministic short-circuit, skip cache-manager, skip telemetry write), **M** (`/gdd:scan`, `/gdd:brief`, `/gdd:sketch`, `/gdd:spike`: current `fast` path), **L** (`/gdd:explore`, `/gdd:discover`, `/gdd:verify`-alone, `/gdd:plan`-alone: current `quick` path), **XL** (`/gdd:next`, `/gdd:do`, autonomous flows, end-to-end Brief→Verify: current `full` path **plus** worktree isolation default + mandatory inter-stage checkpoint + reflector auto-spawn on completion). Router JSON output gains `complexity_class` field; `hooks/budget-enforcer.ts` reads it for class-specific cap enforcement; events.jsonl tags every command for class-specific cost analysis in reflector. **Quality gate (Stage 4.5):** new `skills/quality-gate/SKILL.md` running user-project lint/typecheck/test/visual-regression in parallel between `/gdd:design` and `/gdd:verify`. Detection chain: (1) `.design/config.json#quality_gate.commands` if declared, (2) auto-detect from `package.json#scripts` (match `lint`, `typecheck`/`tsc`, `test` excluding `test:e2e` for speed, `chromatic`, `test:visual`), (3) skip with notice — never blocks. New `agents/quality-gate-runner.md` (Haiku) parses output, classifies failures, decides fix-vs-block. On any failure: spawn `design-fixer` with failure context (already exists from Phase 5); loop until pass or `quality_gate.max_iters` (default 3). Connection-aware — Storybook + Chromatic probe-positive triggers Chromatic baseline-vs-current diff in the report. STATE.md `<quality_gate>` block records per-cycle pass/fail + last-run timestamp. `events.jsonl` emits `quality_gate_*` events. Verify entry refuses to start if gate failed. Configurable `.design/config.json#quality_gate.timeout_seconds` (default 600) — on timeout, gate warns + proceeds rather than blocks (doesn't dominate pipeline on slow test suites). **Turn closeout (Stop hook):** new `hooks/gdd-turn-closeout.js` Stop event handler — fires when assistant turn ends, must be ≤10ms + idempotent + non-blocking. Reads STATE.md (1 file, ~1ms); if `position.status==in_progress` and last events.jsonl entry >60s ago, appends `{event: turn_end, stage, task_progress, ts}`; if stage just completed (`task_progress==N/N`) surfaces nudge "Stage X complete — run /gdd:next or /gdd:reflect", else "Stage X paused mid-task — resume with /gdd:resume". Same logic as portable Skill at `skills/turn-closeout/SKILL.md` for the 13 non-Claude runtimes (codex/gemini/etc. lack a Stop hook surface) — orchestrator skills (`/gdd:next`, `/gdd:design`, `/gdd:verify`) tail-call the skill at exit. Closes the orphan-in-progress problem + auto-routes on stage completion + plugs telemetry gap. **Explicitly out of scope:** auto-running sketch/spike (always confirms — anti-nag rule from spec discussion); changing the 5-stage state machine (prototyping is a checkpoint, not a stage; quality-gate is 4.5, not a renumber); Stop-hook-portability beyond the Skill mirror (mature event-loop-on-turn-end across all 14 runtimes is its own phase); deprecating `fast`/`quick`/`full` (S/M/L/XL is additive — `complexity_class` is a new field alongside `path`, no breaking change for existing consumers). Ships as v1.25.0. **Depends on**: Phase 22 (Stop hook + quality-gate emit typed events into the event chain), Phase 14.5 (decision-injector reads `<prototyping>` block), Phase 23 (solidify-with-rollback composes with quality-gate — solidify is task-level + post-commit, quality-gate is plan-level + pre-verify; both feed events.jsonl).
- [ ] **Phase 26: Headless Model Resolver — Runtime-Aware Tier Mapping** — Closes the model-selection gap left by Phase 24's distribution headlessness. Phase 24 ships the plugin to 14 runtimes (Claude Code, OpenCode, Gemini, Kilo, Codex, Copilot, Cursor, Windsurf, Antigravity, Augment, Trae, Qwen, CodeBuddy, Cline) but every agent's `default-tier: opus|sonnet|haiku` frontmatter is **Anthropic-tier-named** — and the only consumer is `hooks/budget-enforcer.ts`, which is Claude-Code-only. Result: in Codex, every "subagent" runs on whatever single GPT model the user picked for their Codex session — opus-tier planners and haiku-tier checkers collapse to one tier. The router emits `model_tier_overrides` using Anthropic names that no non-CC runtime consumes; `reference/model-prices.md` uses Anthropic prices regardless of runtime; cost telemetry is wrong outside CC. **Tier-to-model adapter layer:** new `reference/runtime-models.md` per-runtime tier→model map (claude → claude-opus-4-7 / claude-sonnet-4-6 / claude-haiku-4-5; codex → gpt-5 / gpt-5-mini / gpt-5-nano; gemini → gemini-2.5-pro / gemini-2.5-flash / gemini-2.5-flash-lite; qwen → qwen3-max / qwen3-plus / qwen3-flash; per-runtime authoritative confirmation required — phase ships the **structure**, not editorial picks). New `scripts/lib/tier-resolver.cjs` exporting `resolve(runtime, tier) → model` with fallback chain (runtime-specific map → runtime-default → null + warning event). `scripts/lib/install/runtimes.cjs` gains `tier_to_model` field per runtime; installer emits a `models.json` per runtime config-dir for runtime harnesses to consume at session start. **Router & telemetry integration:** `skills/router/SKILL.md` emits `resolved_models` field next to `model_tier_overrides` — per-agent concrete model name for the runtime in use; runtime detection via `process.env.CLAUDE_CONFIG_DIR | CODEX_HOME | GEMINI_CONFIG_DIR | …` (same lookup chain Phase 24 installer uses, single source of truth). `hooks/budget-enforcer.ts` (and its non-CC code-level mirrors per Phase 22 primitives) read `resolved_models` for cost computation. `reference/model-prices.md` splits to per-runtime sub-tables (`prices.claude.md`, `prices.codex.md`, `prices.gemini.md`, …); cost telemetry events tag the runtime; reflector class-specific cost analysis works across runtimes (cross-runtime tier-arbitrage becomes a measurable signal — "haiku-tier checkers in Codex actually cost more than sonnet-tier in Claude" surfaces from data, not assumption). **Runtime-neutral abstraction (additive, non-breaking):** `agents/README.md` adds `reasoning-class: high|medium|low` as runtime-neutral alias for `default-tier`; documents the dual mapping (`high → opus|gpt-5|gemini-2.5-pro|qwen3-max`). Existing `default-tier: opus|sonnet|haiku` remains authoritative for v1.26 — the alias lands additively so frontmatter stays back-compat with budget.json `tier_overrides` and Phase 23.5's posterior store. `scripts/validate-frontmatter.ts` gains `reasoning-class` validation; tests assert tier↔class equivalence. Deprecation of `default-tier` in favor of `reasoning-class` is a downstream phase decision once measured usage shows runtime-neutral naming wins (data-gated). **Why this phase exists (research summary):** Phase 24 shipped distribution headlessness (14 runtimes installed) but model-selection headlessness was never delivered. The frontmatter `default-tier: opus` is currently a no-op anywhere outside Claude Code — three layers (agent frontmatter + router + telemetry) all assume Claude. The installer's runtime matrix already distinguishes runtimes; the missing piece is a deterministic tier→model map per runtime that downstream consumers can read. Surfacing this in `runtime-models.md` (vs. hardcoding in `tier-resolver.cjs`) lets runtime adapter authors own the mapping for their runtime — gdd never assumes "GPT-5 is the opus equivalent" without their confirmation. **Explicitly out of scope:** choosing best-fit models per runtime (runtime adapter authors decide; phase ships the **structure** that holds the mapping, not editorial picks — hardcoding equivalences without runtime-author confirmation IS the gap this phase closes; we don't double down on it); per-task model overrides at runtime (Phase 27 territory if measurement shows tier-granularity is insufficient); removing `default-tier` in favor of `reasoning-class` (additive in v1.26 — deprecation is a downstream phase once measured usage shows runtime-neutral naming wins); cross-runtime cost arbitrage in the bandit router (Phase 23.5 posterior is per-(agent, touches-bin) — extending to per-(agent, touches-bin, runtime) is a context-dimension expansion that needs measurement-gated convergence proof first). Ships as v1.26.0. **Depends on**: Phase 24 (runtime matrix in `scripts/lib/install/runtimes.cjs` + per-runtime config-dir lookup chain), Phase 22 (event stream surfaces tier-resolution decisions + runtime-tagged cost events), Phase 23 (JSON output contracts make resolved_models machine-readable for downstream tooling).
- [ ] **Phase 28.5: Skill Authoring Contract + Skill Rework + Project Artifacts (INSERTED)** — Adopts the mattpocock/skills (53,508★, MIT) authoring contract and applies it retroactively across the entire shipped skill set. **The contract**: every SKILL.md ≤100 lines (warn at 100, block at 250); every `description` ≤1024 chars in third-person `<what>. Use when <triggers>.` form; everything else stored via progressive disclosure into `reference/` (or per-skill folder if domain-specific to one skill); `references one level deep` (no nested skill folders); `disable-model-invocation: true` frontmatter for user-invoked-only shortcuts; scripts only when deterministic / repeated / errors-need-explicit-handling. **Skill rework**: every skill in `skills/` (~50+ shipped skills across `gsd-*` pipeline + utility + analysis + `impeccable-*` design family) trimmed to the cap by extracting domain-heavy content into existing `reference/` files (cross-link, don't duplicate) or new `reference/` files when content has no current home. **New artifacts**: `reference/skill-authoring-contract.md` (the contract itself), `reference/context-md-format.md` + `reference/adr-format.md` (ports from mattpocock with MIT attribution + GDD-flavored adaptations), `reference/architecture-vocabulary.md` (Ousterhout's Module/Interface/Implementation/Depth/Seam/Adapter/Leverage/Locality + deletion test). **Project-level artifacts**: `gsd-discuss-phase` + `gsd-spec-phase` gain inline `CONTEXT.md` glossary maintenance (terms get sharpened during interviews; updates land mid-conversation, not batched) and lazy `docs/adr/NNNN-*.md` creation gated on the 3-criteria test (hard-to-reverse AND surprising-without-context AND real-tradeoff). `decision-injector` reads `CONTEXT.md` as project-scoped context (additive to STATE.md cycle-scoped decisions). **Skill patches**: `gsd-debug` Phase 1 adopts the feedback-loop discipline (10-way construction list — failing test → curl → CLI fixture → headless browser → trace replay → throwaway harness → fuzz → bisect → differential → HITL bash — "30-second flaky beats no loop; 2-second deterministic is a debugging superpower"); new `/gdd:zoom-out` micro-skill (~10 lines, `disable-model-invocation: true`, "go up a layer of abstraction, map relevant modules + callers using CONTEXT.md vocabulary"). **Enforcement**: `scripts/validate-skill-length.cjs` runs in CI (warn ≥100 lines, block ≥250; description-length check; frontmatter required-fields check); `gsd-health` includes a skill-length report; regression baseline locks current-best counts. Independent of Phase 28 — touches different files; can land before, after, or in parallel. License-clean: mattpocock/skills is MIT, attribution lands in `NOTICE`. **Depends on**: Phase 14.5 (registry — new reference files register the same way Phase 19.6 used; `decision-injector` extension to read `CONTEXT.md` reuses Phase 14.5 hook plumbing), Phase 15 (foundational references corpus is the destination for extracted skill content), Phase 12 (CI infrastructure that the new validator plugs into). **Out of scope**: TDD-default for executor (separate phase — workflow change requires user buy-in); porting `to-prd` / `to-issues` / `triage` skills (overlap with `gsd-inbox` / `gsd-spec-phase` / connection docs — defer); restructuring all skills into self-contained per-skill folders mattpocock-style (incompatible with GDD's shared `reference/` model — we adopt the contract, keep refs centralized); renaming any skills (rework is content-only, not API-breaking).
- [ ] **Phase 28: Foundational References Tier 2 — Color, Composition, Proportion, i18n** — Closes the fundamentals gap surfaced by the 2026-05-01 huashu-design comparison audit and the parallel i18n-coverage audit: the reference base covers Gestalt + hierarchy + type scale + WCAG 2.1 but has zero coverage of (a) color theory (sRGB/HSL/OKLCH/LCH model differences, hue/chroma/lightness as independent axes, six harmonies — complementary/analogous/triadic/split-complement/tetradic/monochromatic, simultaneous contrast and warm-cool effects, color-blindness-safe palettes for deutan/protan/tritan, color interpolation in animation — OKLCH/Lab vs the sRGB muddy-mid-transition problem); (b) compositional fundamentals (rule of thirds, golden ratio / φ in layout, φ-grid + root rectangles + dynamic symmetry + Fibonacci, focal-point construction, asymmetric balance, optical-vs-mathematical centering, visual-weight calculus — size × contrast × isolation × complexity, eye-flow patterns Z/F/Gutenberg); (c) proportion systems beyond typography (4pt vs 8pt vs root-2 baseline grids, baseline-grid lock + vertical rhythm, modular relationships across type + spacing + sizing + radius — the explicit jump from "modular type scale" to "proportion system across the whole UI"); (d) internationalization fundamentals (text-expansion factors per locale family — DE/FR +30%, RU/FI +40%, JA/ZH −50% — that drive layout constraints; RTL mirroring via CSS logical properties + directional-icon flip rules + bidi isolation; locale formatting via `Intl.DateTimeFormat` / `Intl.NumberFormat` / `Intl.PluralRules` over hand-rolled string concatenation; ICU MessageFormat for plural/select/gender; Unicode hygiene — NFC normalization + grapheme-aware truncation + BCP 47 language tags; multi-script font stacks for CJK/Arabic/Devanagari with `font-display` + subset strategy; WCAG 3.1.1/3.1.2 — `lang` attribute on root + `lang` on language-of-parts). Four new reference files (`reference/color-theory.md`, `reference/composition.md`, `reference/proportion-systems.md`, `reference/i18n.md`) plus optional fifth (`reference/contrast-advanced.md` — APCA / WCAG 3 draft / Lc 75/60/45/30 thresholds / why 4.5:1 misranks thin/large/colored text). Wires via the Phase 14.5 reference registry into existing surfaces — **no new pillar, no new audit dimension, no score-format change**; consumers (impeccable-* family, ultimate-design, gsd-ui-phase, gsd-ui-review, sketch/spike, brief-stage discussant, design-auditor, **design-verifier**) pick up the new references automatically through the retrieval-contract preamble. `design-verifier` gains two i18n-readiness probes (hardcoded-string scan against ICU/i18n-key patterns; layout-overflow check at +40% text-expansion simulation); `skills/explore` gains a design-system i18n-readiness probe (detect `react-intl` / `next-intl` / `i18next` / Vue I18n / native `Intl.*`-only). Cross-links: `color-theory.md` ↔ `palette-catalog.md` Step 4 (replaces "shift hue ±15°" hand-wave with underlying perceptual model) + `motion-interpolate.md` (color-path interpolation guidance); `composition.md` ↔ `visual-hierarchy-layout.md` §Compositional Grids; `proportion-systems.md` ↔ `design-system-guidance.md` + `typography.md` §Modular Scale; `i18n.md` ↔ `typography.md` §Variable Fonts (multi-script font stacks) + `rtl-cjk-cultural.md` (existing RTL/CJK guidance gets a deeper-dive cross-link) + `accessibility.md` §WCAG 2.1/2.2 (lang-of-parts) + `form-patterns.md` (locale-aware input formatting); optional `contrast-advanced.md` ↔ `accessibility.md` §WCAG 2.1/2.2. Purely additive — does not gate any downstream phase. **Depends on**: Phase 14.5 (registry + retrieval-contract preamble that surfaces new references to consumers; same registration path Phase 19.6 used), Phase 15 (foundational references being extended — `palette-catalog.md` + `visual-hierarchy-layout.md` + `design-system-guidance.md`), Phase 18 (`motion-interpolate.md` exists for color-in-motion cross-link), Phase 19 (`rtl-cjk-cultural.md` + `form-patterns.md` exist as i18n.md cross-link surfaces — existing files get deepened, not replaced).
- [ ] **Phase 29: Capability-Gap Telemetry + Self-Authoring of Agents/Skills** — Extends Phase 11 reflector from authoring `reference/*.md` files to also authoring **agents and skills** when capability-gaps recur. New typed event `capability_gap` added to Phase 22 event-chain (emitted at three sources: `/gdd:fast` no-skill-match path, `gdd-router` unmatched-intent path, reflector pattern-detection on repeated `Touches:` clusters without dedicated agent), with fields `{event_id, parent_event_id, source: "fast"|"router"|"reflector_pattern", context_hash, intent_summary, suggested_kind: "agent"|"skill", evidence_refs[]}`. **Two-stage rollout. Stage 0** ships only telemetry — `gdd-events --type capability_gap` filter + reflector aggregates per-cycle gap clusters into a `## Capability gaps observed` section in `.design/reflections/<cycle-slug>.md`; no authoring on Stage 0. **Stage 0 → Stage 1 gate** at `reference/capability-gap-stage-gate.md`: ≥K stable clusters (default K=3) across ≥M cycles (default M=10) with stability defined as Phase 23.5 posterior `stddev(Beta(α, β)) < 0.05`; gate evaluation on every `/gdd:apply-reflections`; surfaces a one-time prompt to enable Stage 1 (user opt-in, never auto-flips). **Stage 1** drafts incubator artifacts at `.design/reflections/incubator/<slug>/` containing `SKILL.md` or `agents/<slug>.md` with Phase 28.5-compliant frontmatter (`name`, `description` in `<what>. Use when <triggers>.` form, `tools`, `default-tier`, optional `reasoning-class`, `parallel-safe`, `reads-only`, `delegate_to: null` defensive default), originating `capability_gap` event refs in a `## Origin` section, computed usage frequency, suggested integration point. `/gdd:apply-reflections` extends with new proposal class — full draft + diff against nearest existing artifact + originating events count + four actions (accept / reject / defer / edit). **Bandit fairness gate** — promoted agents enter Phase 23.5 posterior with conservative `Beta(2, 8)` prior (codified in `posterior-store.cjs` as `prior_class: "promoted_incubator"`) so auto-generated arms don't crowd out proven ones until evidence accumulates. **Incubator TTL** — drafts not promoted/refreshed within P days (default 30) auto-archive via `gsd-cleanup` to `.design/reflections/incubator/archive/<slug>/`; refresh = a new `capability_gap` event matching the existing `context_hash`. **Scope guard** at `scripts/validate-incubator-scope.cjs` blocks promotion outside `agents/` or `skills/` (no runtimes/transports/connections/hooks). Strictly proposal-only — preserves Phase 11 success-criterion-8 "nothing reflector authors auto-ships" discipline. Synergies: `capability_gap` event gains `complexity_class: S|M|L|XL` from Phase 25 router output (separates "missing S-skill" from "missing XL-orchestrator"); incubator frontmatter generated with both `default-tier` and Phase 26 `reasoning-class` so promoted agents are runtime-ready on Codex/Gemini/Qwen; `delegate_to: null` defensive default forward-compats with Phase 27. **Depends on**: Phase 11 (reflector + apply-reflections flow + global skills layer — extension target), Phase 22 (event-chain + redaction primitives — `capability_gap` adds to existing typed schema), Phase 23.5 (posterior store — confidence-interval threshold gates Stage-0→Stage-1 transition + bandit-fairness conservative prior on promoted arms), Phase 14.5 (reference registry — promoted skills register the same way Phase 19.6 used). Soft-coupled to Phases 25/26/27 via additive frontmatter fields — generated artifacts include defensive defaults if soft-deps haven't shipped. **Out of scope**: outbound publication of gap signals (Phase 30 territory); auto-modification of bandit posterior on incubator drafts before promotion; authoring of artifact types beyond agents/skills; deletion proposals for existing agents (additive only); cross-user / opt-in shared capability-gap pool (same rationale as Phase 23.5's deferral of hierarchical Bayesian priors).
- [ ] **Phase 31.5: Repo Structure Consolidation — SDK Folder + npm files Hardening + Distribution Hygiene (INSERTED)** — Closes the three repo-organization regressions surfaced in the 2026-05-04 audit: (a) `.planning/` and `REVIEW.md` are tracked on GitHub despite being in `.gitignore` (12 `.planning/*` files committed before the ignore rule landed; ignore rules don't unstage retroactively); (b) the SDK whose v1.20.0 launch is loudly advertised in `plugin.json` description ("v1.20.0 SDK foundation: gdd-state MCP server, lockfile-safe STATE.md mutations, event stream, resilience primitives") is **physically scattered** — `bin/gdd-sdk` (trampoline), `scripts/lib/cli/` (CLI), `scripts/mcp-servers/gdd-state/` (MCP), `scripts/lib/{jittered-backoff,error-classifier,iteration-budget,lockfile,event-stream,gdd-state,gdd-errors}.cjs` (primitives) sit alongside ~50 unrelated `.cjs` helpers in `scripts/lib/`, with no `sdk/` directory existing; (c) `package.json: files` whitelists `scripts/` wholesale, so the npm tarball ships maintainer-only artifacts (`bootstrap.sh`, `bootstrap-manifest.txt`, `rollback-release.sh`, `apply-branch-protection.sh`, `release-smoke-test.cjs`, `verify-version-sync.cjs`, `extract-changelog-section.cjs`, `detect-stale-refs.cjs`, `run-injection-scanner-ci.cjs`, `injection-patterns.cjs`, `validate-frontmatter.ts`, `validate-schemas.ts`, `e2e/`, `tests/` shell harnesses) to every plugin user. **Three-part fix, all non-breaking at the user-facing API surface (commands, agents, skills, hooks, connections all unchanged).** Part 1 — **stop the leak**: `git rm --cached -r .planning/ REVIEW.md` (files stay on disk locally; subsequent commits don't re-add them); add `tmp_support_preview.png` and any other root-level transients to `.gitignore`; verify `git ls-files | grep -E '^(\.planning/|REVIEW\.md|tmp_)'` returns empty. Part 2 — **collect SDK**: new `sdk/` directory mirrors what `plugin.json` description promises — `sdk/cli/` (from `scripts/lib/cli/`), `sdk/mcp/gdd-state/` (from `scripts/mcp-servers/gdd-state/`), `sdk/state/` (from `scripts/lib/gdd-state/`), `sdk/event-stream/` (from `scripts/lib/event-stream/`), `sdk/primitives/` (from the 4 typed `.cjs` + `.d.cts` pairs: `error-classifier`, `iteration-budget`, `jittered-backoff`, `lockfile` — these have hand-written declarations, marking them as the public-API surface), `sdk/errors/` (from `scripts/lib/gdd-errors/`), `sdk/README.md` (new — documents the public-import contract for SDK consumers). `bin/gdd-sdk` trampoline + `bin/gdd-state-mcp` (new explicit shim instead of pointing `package.json: bin` at a `.ts` file directly) update their relative paths to `../sdk/cli/index.ts` and `../sdk/mcp/gdd-state/server.ts`. **Internal helpers stay put** — `scripts/lib/{adaptive-mode,bandit-router,blast-radius,budget-enforcer,cost-arbitrage,dangerous-patterns,design-search,easings,event-chain,glob-match,mmr-rerank,parse-contract,…}.cjs` are hook/agent-side runtime helpers, NOT public SDK; moving them would inflate scope and risk regressions across hooks. The line is drawn at "what `plugin.json` description names as SDK + what has typed `.d.cts` declarations." Part 3 — **narrow npm tarball**: `package.json: files` rewritten as explicit allowlist — `.claude-plugin/`, `agents/`, `skills/`, `hooks/`, `connections/`, `reference/`, `bin/`, `sdk/`, `scripts/install.cjs` (the only user-facing script — the npm postinstall entry), `scripts/cli/` (existing user-facing CLI dir), `SKILL.md`, `README.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `LICENSE`, `NOTICE`. Drops everything maintainer-only from the tarball. Validated by `npm pack --dry-run` snapshot test in `tests/npm-tarball-contents.test.cjs` (golden file lists every file shipped — diff fails build on accidental additions/removals). **Regression-safety is the dominant concern of this phase, not feature work.** Strict no-data-loss + no-functionality-loss constraints: (i) every move is `git mv` (preserves history), never delete-then-create; (ii) old paths get **shim re-exports** for one minor version (`scripts/lib/cli/index.ts` → `module.exports = require('../../sdk/cli/index.ts')` with a one-time deprecation warning emitted at first import), removed in v1.29.0; (iii) every test in `tests/gdd-sdk-cli.test.ts`, `tests/fixtures/gdd-sdk-cli/`, `tests/agent-size-budget.test.cjs`, and any test that imports from `scripts/lib/{cli,mcp-servers,gdd-state,event-stream,gdd-errors,error-classifier,iteration-budget,jittered-backoff,lockfile}` is re-run against new paths AND old shim paths — both must pass; (iv) `scripts/install.cjs` re-checked against the new file layout (it copies plugin files into `~/.claude/plugins/` so any path it references must update); (v) plugin marketplace install path verified end-to-end via `test-fixture/headless-e2e/` against a freshly packed tarball; (vi) `npm pack --dry-run` output diffed before/after — manifest must shrink monotonically with every dropped path explained in CHANGELOG. **Out of scope** (defer to Phase 31.6+ if needed): rewriting git history to scrub `.planning/` retroactively (history rewrite + force-push needs separate consent and risk review); moving `tests/` or `test-fixture/` out of repo root (they're not in npm `files` anyway, so not leaking to users — only GitHub bloat); publishing `sdk/` as a separate npm package (`@hegemonart/gdd-sdk`) — out of scope for hygiene phase, considered for Phase 32+ if SDK adoption justifies; renaming any commands, skills, agents, hooks (zero-renames discipline preserves muscle memory); deduplicating root-level `AGENTS.md`/`GEMINI.md`/`SKILL.md` (each is a runtime-required convention file). **Target version**: v1.28.0 (minor bump — narrowing npm `files` removes paths from the tarball, which is observable to anyone reaching into `node_modules/@hegemonart/get-design-done/scripts/...` directly; even though no documented interface breaks, semver honesty on tarball contents = minor, not patch). **Depends on**: nothing structural — Phase 31.5 is independent of all in-flight work; can land before Phase 28, 29, 30, 31 or interleaved. Soft-coupled to Phase 31 (Figma extractor lands files in `scripts/lib/figma-extract/` — unaffected; figma-extract is project tooling, not SDK).
- [ ] **Phase 30: Inbound Feedback Channel — Issue Reporter** — Consent-first GitHub issue generator for plugin-level bug reports and feature requests. Closes the user → maintainer feedback loop that today depends on technically-engaged users manually navigating to GitHub — biases reports toward critical bugs, loses long-tail signal. Command `/gdd:report-issue` (and opt-in `--report` flag at command error time, whitelisted) collects local draft with **pseudonymization** (separate layer from Phase 22-12 redaction — Phase 22 scrubs secrets, Phase 30 scrubs identity), shows full payload to user locally, submits via user's own `gh` CLI only on explicit per-issue accept against a hardcoded destination URL. **Pseudonymization** at `scripts/lib/pseudonymize.cjs`: git identity (`user.name`/`user.email` → `<user>`/`<user>@<domain>`), absolute paths (`/Users/X/`/`/home/X/` → `<home>/`), hostname → `<host>`, repo origin URL → `private-org-hash:<sha8>` / `public-personal-hash:<sha8>` (category preserved by `gh` visibility lookup, default `private`), env-vars (`USER`/`LOGNAME`/`HOSTNAME`/`*_TOKEN`/`*_KEY`/`*_SECRET` dropped), email patterns → `<email>`, IP addresses → network-class without last octets. **Stable per-user pseudonym** `sha256(user_id + repo_origin)[:8]` for maintainer-side dedup without identity recovery. **Honest disclaimer** mandatory in both issue body (top section) and TUI consent prompt: "псевдонимизация, не анонимизация — содержимое промптов и кода может косвенно идентифицировать; финальный ревью — на тебе" + English equivalent (text hardcoded, presence-tested). **Security architecture**: destination URL hardcoded in code (no env/config override; immutability-tested constant) → eliminates exfil-redirect attack surface; **no `--yes`/`GDD_AUTO_REPORT=1`** — consent prompt is the only path (any bypass attempt produces explicit error); **payload-on-disk first** at `.design/issue-drafts/<timestamp>-<fingerprint8>.md` with `$EDITOR` review hook (audit trail + DLP-tool interception surface for corporate environments); **outbound = `gh` CLI of the user only** (no plugin-side credentials, no direct HTTPS — CI gate runs static analysis on issue-reporter modules and fails build on any `https://`/`fetch(`/`axios`/`node:https`/`node-fetch` primitive); **kill-switch** via `GDD_DISABLE_ISSUE_REPORTER=1` env or `.design/config.json: { "issue_reporter": false }` (visible in `gsd-health`); **update integrity** via new `/gdd:update --show-privacy-diff` flag showing diff of pseudonymization rules + disclaimer + destination between installed and target versions (auto-shows on first post-upgrade run when relevant files changed). **Pre-submit dedup**: `gh issue list --search "fingerprint:<hash>"` against destination repo (read-only); on match, UI offers `+1` reaction (via `gh api`) or `me-too` comment with minimal added context (last error line + plugin version + runtime) instead of filing duplicate. Fingerprint = `sha256(normalized_stack + command + runtime + plugin_version)`. **Triage gate** before issue prompt: local diagnostics (same class as `gsd-debug`/`gsd-forensics`) check known failure modes catalogued in `reference/known-failure-modes.md`; on match, surface "this looks like X — try Y" without entering issue flow (override via `--force-report` still requires consent prompt). **`gh`-absent fallback**: copies pseudonymized payload to clipboard (`pbcopy`/`xclip`/`clip.exe`) + displays issue-template URL — never silent failure. Synergies: optional outbound channel for Phase 29 `capability_gap` events ("share this gap with maintainers"); single payload pipeline reuses Phase 22-12 redaction + Phase 30 pseudonymization in sequence; runtime-tagging via Phase 22 event-chain `runtime_role` field (if Phase 27 ships) lets maintainers see host vs peer-flow bugs. **Depends on**: Phase 22 (`scripts/lib/redact.cjs` for secrets — Phase 30 layers pseudonymization adjacent, not on top of; event-chain as optional payload source). Soft-coupled to Phase 29 (gap events as optional payload content) and Phase 27 (`runtime_role` tagging if present). **Out of scope**: background telemetry (no daemon, no scheduler, no opt-in pool — `report-issue` is exclusively user-initiated); encrypted/batch submission bypassing `gh`; GDPR-grade anonymization (honest disclaimer, not promised); plugin-side screenshot upload (user attaches manually post-create); NDA-grade trust boundary (kill-switch is the discipline); anonymous third-party submission service; auto-extraction of Phase 11 reflection content into payloads.
- [ ] **Phase 34: Non-Web Output Layer (Native Mobile + Email + Print/PDF)** — Extends GDD past web-only output. Today every executor agent emits React/HTML; Phase 14.7 explicitly defers native, Phase 19 ships platform *references* but zero generators. Phase 34 adds native code generation for SwiftUI / Jetpack Compose / Flutter with shared `reference/native-platforms.md` + token bridge (CSS tokens → SwiftUI `ViewModifier` / Compose `Color`/`MaterialTheme` / Flutter `ThemeData`/`ColorScheme`). Native verify-stage works without DOM via simulator/emulator snapshot capture. Also delivers email-template output (table layout, inline styles, Gmail dark-mode rules; verify via Litmus/Email-on-Acid connection) and PDF/print output (vector tessellation, CMYK awareness, bleed; verify via PDF render-diff). `agents/design-context-builder.md` extends with project-type detection routing brief → web | native | email | print path; `connections/xcode-simulator.md` + `connections/android-emulator.md` + `connections/litmus.md` document setup, probe, and fallback. **Depends on**: Phase 23 (token-engine — shipped), Phase 28 (i18n soft-coupled — RTL/CJK handling propagates to native via shared layer). **Out of scope**: full IDE integration (Xcode/Android Studio plugins), native distribution flows (App Store / Play Store), printer-specific color profiles beyond CMYK awareness.
- [ ] **Phase 35: Audit & Pillar Expansion (Copy + Debt Crawler + Brief Critic + a11y-Gate Hook)** — Closes four audit-side gaps: (a) `design-auditor`'s current 6-pillar model has no copy/UX-writing pillar — Phase 15 brand-voice + Phase 19 form-patterns + Phase 28 i18n give raw material, no scoring; (b) `skills/audit/` is cycle-scoped (reads STATE `<completed_tasks>` for active cycle) but no agent walks an existing legacy codebase first-time-through to enumerate raw colors / antipattern instances / components-without-tokens / contrast violations / density inconsistencies as `.design/debt/DEBT-CATALOG.md`; (c) audit output happens, audit *input* (the brief itself) is never critiqued — vague verbs, missing audience, immeasurable success criteria leak through; (d) Phase 25 quality-gate auto-detects `lint`/`typecheck`/`test`/`chromatic`/`test:visual` but not `axe`/`pa11y`/`lighthouse`, so a11y regressions slip past Stage 4.5. **Delivers**: `agents/copy-auditor.md` + `reference/copy-quality.md` (microcopy / error-messages / empty-states / ARIA-text / alt-text rules) + breaking `design-auditor` 6→7→8 pillar migration with scoring-contract bump (rule #14 closeout discipline applies); `agents/design-debt-crawler.md` (project-wide retroactive, runs from `.design/debt/` not `.design/cycles/<slug>/`) + `reference/debt-categories.md` + priority scoring (visible-delta × effort); `agents/brief-auditor.md` + `reference/brief-quality-rubric.md` (5 anti-patterns: vague verbs, missing audience, immeasurable success, scope creep, missing anti-goals) wired into tail `/gdd:brief`; `hooks/gdd-a11y-gate.js` extending Phase 25 quality-gate's auto-detect list with `axe`/`pa11y`/`lighthouse` + new failure type `a11y` in quality-gate result schema. **Depends on**: Phase 15 (brand-voice), Phase 19 (form-patterns), Phase 25 (quality-gate), Phase 28 (i18n soft-coupled — copy auditor i18n-aware). **Out of scope**: full content design system (style guides, editorial calendars); copy translation workflows (handled by Phase 28 i18n connections, Phase 39 user-research synthesis covers research-driven copy); auto-fixing copy (proposal-only, like reflector — design-fixer doesn't rewrite headlines).
- [ ] **Phase 36: Team Surfaces Layer (PR Inline + Notification Backplane + Ticket Sync)** — Makes GDD visible to teams, not just the engineer running the pipeline. Today `/gdd:ship` creates a PR via `gh` with body assembled from `DESIGN-PLAN.md` + `DESIGN-VERIFICATION.md` + `DESIGN-AUDIT.md`, but verify failures and visual diffs never reach inline PR review surfaces, Slack/Linear/Jira channels, or branch-protection gates. **Delivers**: `agents/pr-commenter.md` posts inline review comments via `gh api` (selector-specific WCAG violations + Phase 8 Preview/Chromatic before-after screenshot pairs as image attachments); `gh check create` registers `gdd/design-review` as a status check integrated with branch protection rules; `connections/slack.md` + `linear.md` + `jira.md` + `discord.md` follow the Phase 14 connection-doc template + capability matrix gains "notify" + "ticket-sync" columns; `agents/ticket-sync-agent.md` does bidirectional Linear/Jira ticket ↔ DESIGN.md status (decision-injector reads ticket comments on `.design/**.md` open; design-stage writes `<ticket_links>` STATE block); all outbound calls route through Phase 22 redact.cjs + Phase 30 pseudonymize.cjs (privacy guard, no raw secrets/identity leaks). **Depends on**: Phase 22 (event-chain + redact), Phase 25 (Chromatic in quality-gate provides baseline-vs-current diff payload for PR screenshots), Phase 30 (pseudonymize.cjs reuse for non-pseudonymized-by-default outbound channels). Soft-coupled to Phase 27 (`runtime_role` tagging in notification payloads for peer-flow attribution). **Out of scope**: full bug-tracker integration (not just status sync — issue creation/triage stays in Phase 30 territory); video walkthroughs in PR comments (still images via Chromatic only); design-review approval workflow beyond status check (no GDD-side approver list).
- [ ] **Phase 37: Knowledge Tier 3 (Domain Packs + Motion-Tool Verification + Conversational UI)** — Closes three remaining reference-side gaps. Domain side: Phase 16/17 ship 18 generic design systems, Phase 28 ships color/composition/proportion/i18n, but no **industry-specific** patterns — finance (data tables, trading interfaces, regulatory disclaimer placement), healthcare (HIPAA-aware forms, PHI isolation patterns, MyChart-class flows), gaming (HUD/diegetic UI, high-motion accessibility, ESRB age-gates), civic/government (Section 508, multi-language gov forms, accessibility-first defaults). Motion side: Phase 18 ships motion *principles* (Disney 12, motion vocabulary, FLIP/View-Transitions), but no runtime player verification — Lottie + Rive exports flow through pipelines unchecked. Conversational side: bot/voice/prompt-as-UX flows are zero-coverage today even though they're a real product surface. **Delivers**: `reference/domains/finance-patterns.md` + `healthcare-patterns.md` + `gaming-patterns.md` + `civic-patterns.md` wired into `design-context-builder` (domain detection from brief) + `design-auditor` (domain-specific checklist additions); `connections/lottie.md` + `connections/rive.md` + `agents/motion-verifier.md` (loads exported animation, validates state-machine graph + performance budget on motion bundle KB); `reference/conversational-ui.md` (voice flows, multi-turn dialogue, prompt-as-UX, chatbot empty-states, voice-first onboarding). **Depends on**: Phase 18 (motion refs — shipped), Phase 19 (platforms — shipped), Phase 28 (i18n — planned, civic-patterns needs RTL/multi-script). **Out of scope**: full domain certification workflows (HIPAA compliance is a legal process, not a checklist; we surface patterns + flag risks, not certify); proprietary trading platform integrations (Bloomberg Terminal, etc.); voice synthesis (TTS quality / SSML grading) — text-side only.
- [ ] **Phase 38: AI-Native Tools Wave 2 + Greenfield Design System Bootstrap** — Extends Phase 14's AI-native design-tool layer with the six tools backlogged in `connections/connections.md` (Framer, Penpot, Webflow, v0.dev, Plasmic, Builder.io Visual Copilot) under the existing capability contract (canvas | generator | shared probe). Each ships a connection doc + capability-matrix row; component-generator implementations follow Phase 14's `agents/component-generator.md` `<!-- impl: -->` tagged section pattern. Plus closes the greenfield gap — today GDD assumes a design system exists in code or in Figma; Phase 38 ships `skills/bootstrap-ds/SKILL.md` entry point + `agents/ds-generator.md` (brand-input → token-system: color tints/shades from primary, modular type-scale, geometric spacing-scale, motion-defaults, radius-scale) + `reference/ds-bootstrap-rubric.md` + first-component scaffolding (button/input/card in detected target framework as proof artifact). The Phase 16/17 benchmark corpus is the reference DNA for greenfield generation — agent doesn't invent, it adapts established conventions. **Depends on**: Phase 14 (AI-native tool contract — shipped), Phase 23 (token-engine — shipped), Phase 16/17 (benchmark corpus — shipped). **Out of scope**: bespoke brand identity systems (logomarks, brand guidelines beyond color + type — handoff to Phase 15 brand-voice); Penpot self-hosting setup (we connect to user's instance, we don't install Penpot); Webflow-specific CMS modeling (we read structure, not author CMS schemas).
- [ ] **Phase 39: Outcome-Driven Adaptation (A/B Variants + Inbound User-Research Signals)** — Closes the external-outcome loop: today Phase 19.5 archives per-cycle EXPERIENCE.md, Phase 23.5 learns from solidify-gate outcomes, Phase 27.5 wires bandit into production routing — but the bandit's reward signal is **internal** (lint/test/visual diff pass/fail), not user-facing (did this design actually win in A/B? did users complete the flow? did support tickets drop?). Phase 39 adds two external signal sources. **A/B variants:** `design-stage --variants N` mode generates N design variants tagged with hypotheses; `connections/launchdarkly.md` + `statsig.md` + `growthbook.md` ingest experiment results via `agents/experiment-result-ingester.md`; results feed Phase 23.5 posterior store as a *new arm class* (`design_arms`, distinct from `routing_arms`) — the bandit learns which design patterns win, not just which model tier is cost-effective. **User research:** `connections/usertesting.md` + `maze.md` + `hotjar.md` + `agents/user-research-synthesizer.md` reads session-replays / test-reports / feedback streams → brief-grade insights; brief stage gains `<prior-research>` block populated from prior cycles + current connection state; verify stage gains cross-check ("does this design address findings X, Y, Z from latest UserTesting study?"). All PII routed through Phase 30 pseudonymize.cjs. **Depends on**: Phase 23.5 (posterior store extension — shipped), Phase 22 (event-chain for ingester emissions — shipped), Phase 30 (pseudonymize.cjs — planned). **Out of scope**: A/B test orchestration (we read results, we don't run experiments — LaunchDarkly/Statsig/GrowthBook stay primary surface for experiment lifecycle); session-replay video storage (we read indexed insights, not raw recordings); causal inference beyond correlation (we report what won, we don't claim attribution).
- [ ] **Phase 40: Ops & Migration (Design-System Migration Workflows + Long-Horizon Cost Governance)** — Closes two long-tail operational gaps. **DS migration:** when shadcn v1→v2, Tailwind v3→v4, MUI v5→v6, or Material 3→4 land breaking changes, today users hand-migrate; Phase 13.3 plugin-update-checker only handles GDD self-updates, not user DS upgrades. Delivers `agents/ds-migration-planner.md` + `reference/migrations/{shadcn-v2,tailwind-v4,mui-v6,material-3-to-4}.md` per-DS migration rule libraries + codemod generator (jscodeshift / ast-grep templates) + per-component impact scoring (visual delta × component usage frequency × tests-affected) + verify-stage migration validation (contract preserved + no unintended visual regressions). **Cost governance:** Phase 10.1 ships per-task caps, Phase 26 ships per-runtime cost telemetry, Phase 27.5 wires bandit cost-arbitrage into routing — but no *project-level* forecast or hard-halt. Delivers `skills/budget/SKILL.md` (`/gdd:budget` forecasts next-N-cycles cost from costs.jsonl + events.jsonl + EXPERIENCE outcomes) + `agents/cost-forecaster.md` + `budget.json.project_cap` config + hard-halt hook (blocks pipeline when project burns past cap) + ROI dashboard (cost × accepted-vs-reverted from git history — finally tells the user "this cycle cost $X and shipped Y commits that stuck"). **Depends on**: Phase 13.3 (update-checker architecture — shipped), Phase 19.5 (EXPERIENCE outcomes — shipped), Phase 23 (token-engine for migration diff — shipped), Phase 26 (per-runtime cost — shipped), Phase 27.5 (bandit cost-arbitrage — planned). **Out of scope**: design-system upgrades not catalogued in the rule library (long-tail user DS systems — provide template for users to author their own migration rule); auto-applying migrations without consent (proposal-only, user reviews per-component); cost prediction at agent-call granularity (forecast is cycle-scoped, not call-scoped).
- [ ] **Phase 41: Team Collaboration Mode** — Architectural phase opening multi-developer collaboration. Today Phase 20 lockfile + atomic STATE.md RMW give single-process safety; multi-developer concurrent design work is unsupported — STATE.md assumes one author, DESIGN.md decisions are linear, no async review queue, no shared decision journal visible to PMs/designers who don't run GDD locally. **Delivers**: CRDT or OT model for STATE.md `<decisions>` + DESIGN.md sections (or alternative — git-merge-driver per-section with semantic conflict detection); `agents/conflict-resolver.md` for design-artifact merge conflicts across branches; PR-comment workflow on DESIGN.md (comments link to D-XX decisions, threaded discussion stays attached to decision history); shared decision-journal export to Notion / Confluence (read-only, regenerated on cycle close); multi-author attribution in STATE.md `<decisions>` blocks; `gdd-state` MCP server gains multi-writer semantics (Phase 20 lockfile extends to coordinated multi-process writes); async review queue at `.design/reviews/<decision-id>/` with per-decision approval state; sectional handoff mode (designer-mode = Brief + Explore in Figma, dev-mode = Plan + Design + Verify in code — typed at cycle start, drives stage-skip permissions); cross-machine state sync option via S3 / git-LFS backend; permission model (who can write which sections / which decisions are locked once shipped). **Depends on**: Phase 20 (lockfile — shipped), Phase 22 (event-chain for attribution — shipped), Phase 30 (pseudonymize.cjs for outbound Notion/Confluence — planned). **Out of scope**: real-time collaboration UI (we ship semantics + git workflow, not Figma-multiplayer-style live cursors); SSO / SAML integration (we use existing git auth + Notion/Confluence's own auth); GDD-side user management (users are git authors).

## Phase Details

### Phase 1: Foundation + Distribution + Infrastructure
**Goal**: Plugin repo is clean for user distribution, bash patterns are cross-platform, an explicit state machine exists, and the agents/ + connections/ scaffolding is in place for Phase 2
**Depends on**: Nothing (first phase)
**Requirements**: DIST-01, DIST-02, DIST-03, PLAT-01, PLAT-02, PLAT-03, PLAT-04, STATE-01, STATE-02, STATE-03, AGENT-00, CONN-00, SCAN-04
**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE):
  1. Fresh `git clone` of the plugin repo contains no `.planning/`, no `.claude/memory/`, no `.claude/settings.local.json` — the user gets only what the plugin distributes
  2. Running any pipeline stage on macOS or Windows Git Bash produces the same grep match counts as on Linux (no silent false-negatives)
  3. `.gitattributes` enforces LF line endings and `git status` shows no unexpected diffs after checkout on Windows
  4. `.design/STATE.md` is initialized after scan; all subsequent stages read and update it — a killed session resumes from the last checkpoint
  5. `agents/README.md` and `connections/connections.md` exist and define the conventions for Phase 2+
**Plans**: 5 plans (1 gap closure)

Plans:
- [ ] 01-01-PLAN.md — Distribution cleanup: .gitignore additions, untrack .planning/ and .claude/memory/, README Distribution section (DIST-01/02/03)
- [ ] 01-02-PLAN.md — Cross-platform bash: .gitattributes LF enforcement, bootstrap.sh Windows path normalization, POSIX grep migration in scan+verify SKILL.md, SCAN-04 source-root fallback (PLAT-01/02/03/04, SCAN-04)
- [ ] 01-03-PLAN.md — State machine template: reference/STATE-TEMPLATE.md with XML sections and write contract (STATE-01/02/03)
- [ ] 01-04-PLAN.md — Infrastructure scaffolding: agents/README.md authoring contract, connections/connections.md capability matrix, git mv refero.md → connections/ (AGENT-00, CONN-00)
- [ ] 01-05-PLAN.md — Gap closure: migrate 6 residual grep -rn patterns in scan/verify SKILL.md to POSIX ERE with -E flag + POSIX word-boundary replacement (PLAT-02, re-opened)

### Phase 2: Core Agents + Stage Orchestration
**Goal**: The pipeline runs through specialized agents — discover/plan/design/verify become thin orchestrators that spawn the right agent for each sub-task, matching GSD's planner/executor/verifier pattern
**Depends on**: Phase 1 (needs state machine + agent scaffolding)
**Requirements**: AGENT-01, AGENT-02, AGENT-03, AGENT-04, AGENT-05, STAGE-01, STAGE-02, STAGE-03, STAGE-04
**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE):
  1. All 5 core agents exist in `agents/` with complete frontmatter (name, description, tools, color), required_reading sections, and documented completion markers
  2. `plan` stage spawns design-phase-researcher (optional per config) + design-planner + design-plan-checker and no longer inlines task decomposition in the skill
  3. `design` stage spawns design-executor per task with wave coordination; each task produces an atomic git commit and a `.design/tasks/task-NN.md`
  4. `verify` stage spawns design-verifier which iterates (gaps → fix → re-verify) instead of linear 5-phase execution
  5. End-to-end pipeline still works on a test project — no regressions vs v2.1.0 behavior
**Plans**: 4 plans

Plans:
- [x] 02-01-PLAN.md — design-planner + design-phase-researcher + design-plan-checker agents, plan stage orchestrator rewrite (AGENT-01, AGENT-04, AGENT-05, STAGE-02)
- [x] 02-02-PLAN.md — design-executor agent + design stage orchestrator rewrite with wave coordination and atomic commits (AGENT-02, STAGE-03)
- [ ] 02-03-PLAN.md — design-verifier agent + verify stage orchestrator rewrite with gap-response loop (AGENT-03, STAGE-04)
- [ ] 02-04-PLAN.md — discover minimal STATE.md wrapper + end-to-end smoke test on fixture (STAGE-01)

### Phase 3: Quality Gate Agents + Pipeline Polish
**Goal**: Six quality-gate agents are integrated into the pipeline and every known rough edge in the polish backlog is resolved — the pipeline produces accurate results for Next.js App Router, Remix, SvelteKit, and Tailwind-only projects
**Depends on**: Phase 2 (quality gates plug into agent-orchestrated stages)
**Requirements**: AGENT-06, AGENT-07, AGENT-08, AGENT-09, AGENT-10, AGENT-11, SCAN-01, SCAN-02, SCAN-03, DISC-01, DISC-02, DISC-03, PLAN-01, PLAN-02, DSGN-01, DSGN-02, DSGN-03, VRFY-01, VRFY-02, REF-01, REF-02, REF-03, REF-04, REF-05
**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE):
  1. `discover` spawns design-context-builder → design-context-checker; DESIGN-CONTEXT.md is approved before planning begins
  2. `verify` spawns design-auditor (6 pillars scored 1–4) + design-integration-checker (wiring verification) as part of its iterative loop
  3. Running scan on a Next.js App Router project (no `src/`) produces a valid DESIGN.md with component inventory — no empty sections
  4. Running discover on a Tailwind-only project (no CSS files) completes without error and audits Tailwind config instead of CSS grep
  5. Brownfield project: design-pattern-mapper surfaces existing colors/spacing/components before planning so plan doesn't conflict with established patterns
  6. All five reference files contain the new content sections (archetypes, variable fonts, spring physics, scroll-triggered animations, Visual Hierarchy grep patterns)
**Plans**: 5 plans

Plans:
- [ ] 03-01: design-context-builder + design-context-checker + discover orchestrator update
- [ ] 03-02: design-auditor + design-integration-checker + verify orchestrator update
- [ ] 03-03: design-pattern-mapper + design-assumptions-analyzer + plan orchestrator update
- [ ] 03-04: Scan polish — component detection, --full mode, DESIGN-DEBT ordering
- [ ] 03-05: Plan + design + verify polish — task templates, --research doc, execution guides, oklch, decision authority, VISUAL flags
- [ ] 03-06: Reference file expansions — audit-scoring, typography archetypes + variable fonts, motion spring physics + scroll-triggered

### Phase 4: Connections Layer
**Goal**: Figma and Refero MCPs are first-class connections with documented setup, graceful fallback, and a documented pattern for adding future connections (Storybook, Linear, GitHub)
**Depends on**: Phase 3 (connections are invoked from agent-orchestrated stages)
**Requirements**: CONN-01, CONN-02, CONN-03, CONN-04, CONN-05, CONN-06
**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE):
  1. `connections/figma.md` + `connections/refero.md` document setup, per-tool capabilities, and fallback behavior — a new user can enable either connection by following the guide
  2. Scan stage reads Figma variables when Figma MCP is available and logs the source in DESIGN.md; falls back to code-only analysis when not
  3. Discover stage pre-populates `<decisions>` from Figma and `<references>` from Refero when available; completes without either
  4. `connections/connections.md` capability matrix shows which stages use which connection and includes an extensibility guide for adding a new connection
  5. Every stage records in STATE.md which connections were active during that run — a reader can trace which outputs came from which source
**Plans**: 3 plans

Plans:
- [ ] 04-01-PLAN.md — Connection documentation + canonical availability probe (connections/figma.md NEW, connections/refero.md + connections.md UPDATE) (CONN-01, CONN-02, CONN-06)
- [ ] 04-02-PLAN.md — Figma MCP wiring: scan State Integration + Step 2A Token Augmentation; design-context-builder Step 0 Pre-population (CONN-03, CONN-04)
- [ ] 04-03-PLAN.md — Refero MCP wiring: design-context-builder Area 5 with three-tier fallback (Refero → awesome-design-md → WebFetch); discover/SKILL.md concrete probe queries (CONN-05)

### Phase 5: Automation Agents + New Commands
**Goal**: Three automation agents (fixer, advisor, doc-writer) close the verify→fix loop, handle gray-area research, and generate handoff docs — and three new commands (style, darkmode, compare) ship using them
**Depends on**: Phase 3 (automation agents are invoked by the pipeline + new commands); Phase 4 optional (commands work without connections but benefit from them)
**Requirements**: AGENT-12, AGENT-13, AGENT-14, STYL-01, STYL-02, STYL-03, STYL-04, STYL-05, DARK-01, DARK-02, DARK-03, DARK-04, DARK-05, DARK-06, DARK-07, COMP-01, COMP-02, COMP-03, COMP-04, COMP-05
**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE):
  1. design-verifier + design-fixer close the verify→fix loop automatically — a gap in DESIGN-VERIFICATION.md is resolved without the user re-planning
  2. design-advisor produces a comparison table for any gray area flagged in discover — replaces "user best guess" with researched trade-offs
  3. `@get-design-done style Button` invokes design-doc-writer and produces `.design/DESIGN-STYLE-Button.md` with all required token sections (works post-pipeline and pre-pipeline)
  4. `@get-design-done darkmode` detects dark mode architecture, runs the audit, and produces `.design/DARKMODE-AUDIT.md` with a P0–P3 fix list
  5. `@get-design-done compare` produces `.design/COMPARE-REPORT.md` with per-category delta, anti-pattern delta, and design-drift flagging
  6. None of the new commands pollute the pipeline artifact namespace — all use distinct prefixes
**Plans**: 5 plans

Plans:
- [x] 05-01-PLAN.md — design-fixer agent + integrate into verify loop
- [ ] 05-02-PLAN.md — design-advisor agent + integrate into discover gray-area resolution
- [ ] 05-03-PLAN.md — design-doc-writer agent + style command (SKILL.md, two modes, router update)
- [ ] 05-04-PLAN.md — darkmode command — SKILL.md, architecture detection, audit checks, router update
- [ ] 05-05-PLAN.md — compare command — SKILL.md, delta logic, drift detection, router update

### Phase 6: Validation + Version Bump
**Goal**: The plugin passes formal validation, all commands work on a real Windows Git Bash project, and ships as get-design-done **v1.0.0** (version reset on rename — legacy ultimate-design was v3.0.0).
**Depends on**: Phases 4 and 5
**Requirements**: VAL-01, VAL-02, VAL-03
**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE):
  1. `claude plugin validate .` exits 0 with no errors or warnings after all v3 changes
  2. Root SKILL.md argument-hint frontmatter, Command Reference table, and Jump Mode section all list style, darkmode, and compare — invoking any of them routes correctly
  3. `.claude-plugin/plugin.json` and `.claude-plugin/marketplace.json` both show version `1.0.0` (rename reset; ultimate-design legacy was v3.0.0)
  4. `claude plugin install hegemonart/get-design-done` on a fresh Claude Code instance installs cleanly and the pipeline runs end-to-end
**Status**: ✓ COMPLETE (2026-04-18)
**Plans**: 1 plan

- [x] 06-01-PLAN.md — Rename to get-design-done, reset version to 1.0.0 (plugin.json + marketplace.json; legacy ultimate-design was v3.0.0), description refresh, validate both manifests (VAL-01, VAL-02, VAL-03)

### Phase 7: GSD Parity + Exploration — Discussant, Ergonomics, Sketch/Spike, Architecture Uplift
**Goal**: Close the GSD parity gap AND ship exploration-before-commit. Design decisions are gathered through adaptive questioning (not a fixed script), the pipeline is navigable via explicit state commands, codebase mapping runs in parallel through scoped agents, the plugin supports multi-cycle design work, and designers can explore directions via `/gdd:sketch` (multi-variant HTML) and `/gdd:spike` (design feasibility experiments) with wrap-up flows that codify findings as project-local skills auto-loaded on every future session.
**Depends on**: Phase 6 (stable v1.0.0 baseline). Can run in parallel with Phase 8 (see "Parallelization" at end of roadmap).
**Requirements**: GSD-01 through GSD-20, SKT-01 through SKT-04, SPK-01 through SPK-04, PLS-01 through PLS-04 (to be defined during plan-phase)

**Scope discipline (post-critique trims — 2026-04-18):**

Items explicitly **dropped** to keep the phase coherent:
- `/gdd:insert-stage`, `/gdd:remove-stage` — premature; no demonstrated need; the 5-stage pipeline has been stable since v1
- Standalone `/gdd:spec-phase` command — Socratic refinement + ambiguity scoring fold into the discussant as a mode (`/gdd:discuss --spec` or the discussant detecting ambiguity internally). Avoids four overlapping question-asking mechanisms.

Items **restored** after initial dropping:
- `/gdd:reapply-patches` — originally deferred as premature; restored to Wave A plan 07-03b because it must ship with `/gdd:update` (update without reapply clobbers user `reference/` tweaks).

Items explicitly **consolidated**:
- `/gdd:todo` + `/gdd:check-todos` → one `/gdd:todo` command with subcommands (`add`, `list`, `pick`)
- `/gdd:audit-cycle` + `/gdd:validate-cycle` → one `/gdd:audit` command with `--retroactive` flag for validation mode
- `/gdd:set-profile` → moved under `/gdd:settings profile <name>` (not a standalone command)
- `/gdd:cleanup` → moved under `/gdd:settings cleanup` (not a standalone command)

Net command count: **24 → 17 new commands in this phase**. Remaining: discuss, progress, health, todo, settings, map, audit, pause, resume, new-cycle, debug, quick, sketch, sketch-wrap-up, spike, spike-wrap-up, plus flags on existing commands.

**Wave structure — three ship checkpoints:**

Phase 7 merges to `main` **three times**, at the end of each wave. If priorities shift mid-phase, any wave boundary is a clean stopping point with shippable functionality.

| Wave | Plans | Ships | Dependency out |
|------|-------|-------|----------------|
| **A — Foundation** | 07-00, 07-01, 07-02, 07-02b, 07-03, 07-03b, 07-08 | Pipeline reshape + `/gdd:` namespace + `/gdd:help`; discussant (evolved from context-builder) + `/gdd:list-assumptions`; progress/health/todo/stats (with `--forensic`); idea capture layer (note/plant-seed/backlog/review-backlog); settings schema (model_profile + parallelism); maintenance commands (`/gdd:update` + `/gdd:reapply-patches`); agent hygiene + injection scanner + parallel-safety frontmatter | Plugin runs on canonical pipeline shape with new discussant; decision-engine data in place; full ergonomics layer; users can upgrade safely |
| **B — Architecture** | 07-04, 07-04b, 07-05, 07-06, 07-06b, 07-07 | 5 mappers (2 splits + 3 new); wave-native pipeline (decision engine live across all stages); research synthesizer; `/gdd:audit` wrapping existing verifier/auditor; cycle layer; pause/resume/debug/quick; lifecycle commands (new-project/complete-cycle/fast); workflow router + ship + undo + pr-branch | Architecture final — sketch/spike can plug in cleanly; verify→ship loop closed |
| **C — Exploration + Closeout** | 07-09, 07-10, 07-11, 07-12 | Sketch + spike commands with their own integration hooks; project-local skills + CLAUDE.md auto-load + required_reading extensions; phase closeout (version bump, README/manifest refresh, CHANGELOG, baseline lock) | Phase 7 complete at v1.0.1 |

**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE, grouped by wave):

*After Wave A:*
  1. `/gdd:discuss [topic]` spawns `design-discussant` (evolved from `design-context-builder`, with detection stripped out) — asks one question at a time, adapts, writes numbered D-XX decisions to STATE.md `<decisions>` block (no new DECISIONS.md artifact). Stops when sufficient for planning. `--all` batches gray areas; `--spec` adds ambiguity scoring on top of normal questioning. Parallel discuss supported across independent cycles.
  2. `discover` stage orchestrator invokes `design-discussant` as its first step; interview logic in `skills/discover/SKILL.md` is removed from the skill.
  3. `/gdd:progress` reads STATE.md and routes to next action. `--forensic` flag runs a 6-check integrity audit (stale artifacts, missing transitions, token drift, aged DESIGN-DEBT, cycle alignment, connection status).
  4. `/gdd:health` reports `.design/` state — stale DESIGN.md vs code mtime, missing artifacts, token drift, aged DESIGN-DEBT entries, broken state transitions.
  5. `/gdd:todo <add|list|pick>` captures, lists, and picks backlog items.
  6. `.design/config.json` exposes full schema: `model_profile` (quality/balanced/budget) + `parallelism` object (enabled, max_parallel_agents, min_tasks_to_parallelize, min_estimated_savings_seconds, require_disjoint_touches, worktree_isolation, per_stage_override). `/gdd:settings` command supports `profile <name>`, `parallelism <key> <value>`, `cleanup` subcommands.
  7. Every agent's frontmatter declares `parallel-safe: always|never|conditional-on-touches`, `typical-duration-seconds`, `reads-only`, and `writes` — the data the decision engine reads in Wave B.
  8. Agent size-budget enforced per role (line-count tiers); boilerplate extracted to `@file` includes across all 14+ agents. `gdd-read-injection-scanner` PostToolUse hook active.
  8a. `/gdd:update` pulls latest release, re-syncs plugin files, preserves `.design/config.json` + `./.claude/skills/`. `/gdd:reapply-patches` reapplies user modifications to `reference/` against pristine baseline via git diff. Both ship together; update is safe to run without losing local customizations.

*After Wave B:*
  9. `/gdd:map` dispatches 5 mappers — 2 from splitting existing `design-pattern-mapper` (`token-mapper`, `component-taxonomy-mapper`) + 3 new (`visual-hierarchy-mapper`, `a11y-mapper`, `motion-mapper`). Each writes one doc under `.design/map/`. Scan stage consumes these instead of running serial grep.
  10. **Wave-native pipeline**: every skill orchestrator (scan, discover, plan, design, verify) uses the parallelism decision engine (reads settings + rules + agent data, writes verdict to STATE.md `<parallelism_decision>`). `reference/parallelism-rules.md` codifies hard rules (sequential dep, shared write, interactive agent, single task, overlapping Touches) and soft rules (est-savings threshold, fast-agent bias, wave-cap splitting). Parallel-when-needed, not reflexively.
  11. `design-research-synthesizer` consumes phase-researcher + mappers + connections (Figma/Refero/Pinterest/Storybook) + discussant output → unified `DESIGN-CONTEXT.md`.
  12. `/gdd:audit` is a command wrapping existing `design-verifier` + `design-auditor` — no new agent. `--retroactive` invokes verifier with cycle-span scope.
  13. `/gdd:pause` writes a handoff; `/gdd:resume` restores context. Killed mid-cycle sessions restart without re-running completed stages.
  14. `/gdd:new-cycle` creates a cycle; STATE.md `cycle:` frontmatter field is active; `.design/CYCLES.md` tracks. Pipeline runs scope to the active cycle. Hierarchy is explicit: Cycle > Run > Wave > Task.
  15. `/gdd:debug` starts a symptom-driven investigation with persistent state; `reference/debugger-philosophy.md` codifies the approach. `/gdd:quick` runs the pipeline with optional agents skipped.

*After Wave C:*
  16. `/gdd:sketch [topic]` creates `.design/sketches/<slug>/` with intake + N standalone HTML variants (default 3). `--quick` bypasses intake. No `/gdd:new-project` prerequisite. Integration hooks ship with this plan: scan detects prior sketches, planner includes findings in `<files_to_read>`, design-stage offers sketch as a route when directionally open.
  17. `/gdd:sketch-wrap-up` walks sketches, elicits winner + rationale, groups by design area, writes project skills to `./.claude/skills/design-<area>-conventions.md`. Summary in `.design/sketches/SUMMARY.md`.
  18. `/gdd:spike [question]` creates `.design/spikes/<slug>/` with question + throwaway artifact + findings log. `--quick` bypasses intake. Integration hooks ship with this plan: scan detects prior spikes, planner includes findings, verify surfaces pending exploration.
  19. `/gdd:spike-wrap-up` codifies findings into `./.claude/skills/design-<topic>-findings.md`; summary in `.design/spikes/SUMMARY.md`.
  20. Project-local skills at `./.claude/skills/` auto-load via routing injected into project CLAUDE.md. Discussant, planner, and executor `<required_reading>` blocks extended to include `./.claude/skills/*.md`. Future gdd invocations inherit codified decisions — no re-asking. `/gdd:progress` surfaces pending sketch/spike work; `/gdd:pause` captures active sketch/spike context in handoff.
  21. Sketch variants render as standalone HTML (no build step) — browser-openable directly, screenshot-able by Phase 8 preview/playwright later. Artifacts usable without Phase 8.

**Architectural principles applied (post-critique, 2026-04-18):**

1. **Discussant evolves `design-context-builder`, not a new agent.** Current builder does both detection + interview — two jobs. Split: detection → `design-pattern-mapper` (exists) + Wave B specialist mappers; interview → rename/narrow builder to `design-discussant`.
2. **Mappers: 2 splits + 3 new, not 5 new from scratch.** Split existing `design-pattern-mapper` → `token-mapper` + `component-taxonomy-mapper`; add `visual-hierarchy-mapper`, `a11y-mapper`, `motion-mapper`.
3. **`/gdd:audit` is a command wrapping existing `design-verifier` + `design-auditor`, not a new agent.** `--retroactive` flag invokes verifier with cycle-span scope.
4. **DECISIONS.md does not exist as a new artifact.** STATE.md `<decisions>` block already has D-XX numbering — discussant writes there. One source of truth.
5. **Hierarchy pinned**: `Cycle` (goal) > `Pipeline run` (scan→verify) > `Wave` (parallel batch) > `Task` (atomic commit). STATE.md gains a `cycle:` frontmatter field.
6. **Plan 07-07 dissolved**: `--forensic` → into 07-02; parallel discuss → into 07-01; injection scanner → into 07-08.
7. **Plan 07-12 dissolved**: integration hooks ship with their respective Wave C plans (07-09/10/11).
8. **New plan 07-04b — Wave-native pipeline**: parallelism is **computed** (from settings × rules × data), not specified per task. Every stage orchestrator uses the decision engine.

**Parallelism: settings + rules, not reflex**

Parallelism is a first-class architectural primitive, not a per-task flag. See plans 07-03, 07-04b, and 07-08 for where it lives:

- **Settings** (`.design/config.json` → `parallelism` object; user-tunable via `/gdd:settings parallelism ...`):
  - `enabled`, `max_parallel_agents`, `min_tasks_to_parallelize`, `min_estimated_savings_seconds`, `require_disjoint_touches`, `worktree_isolation`, `per_stage_override`
- **Rules** (`reference/parallelism-rules.md` — hard + soft):
  - Hard: sequential dependency, shared writes, interactive agent, single task, overlapping `Touches:` → serial
  - Soft: below est-savings threshold, all candidates fast (<10s), beyond cap → prefer serial or split into waves
- **Data** (declarative, read by decision engine):
  - Agent frontmatter: `parallel-safe: always|never|conditional-on-touches`, `typical-duration-seconds`, `reads-only`, `writes`
  - Plan `Touches:` field (already exists) is the load-bearing signal for independence

Every orchestrator spawn point calls the decision engine and writes its verdict to STATE.md `<parallelism_decision>` so "why didn't it parallelize?" is a one-file read, not a guess.

**Plans**: 17 plans across 3 waves (7 Wave A + 6 Wave B + 4 Wave C)
